***dauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dauw.html>dauw</a> (23878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dau.html>dau</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dāu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dawwaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke, haze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:dau.html>Dau</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:dau.html>dau</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tau.html>Tau</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dew</i>, compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">dug</i>.

***daverend.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:daverend.html>daverend</a> (30002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daverend.html>daverend</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">daverender</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">daverendst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>resounding, tremendous, enormous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Sanders <a href = vnd.unilang:behaalde.html>behaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b>daverende</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:overwinning.html>overwinning</a> in Nevada.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Sanders obtained a <b>resounding</b> victory in Nevada.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Used mainly attributively, in particular with nouns denoting success, applause or laughter.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of success</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinkend.html>klinkend</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of laughter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulderend.html>bulderend</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daverend.html>daverend</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">daveren</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:daverend.html>daverend</a></b>
</p>

***dazzle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a> (65497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:daas.html>daze</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-le</i>, a frequentative form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">dazzles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dazzling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dazzled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To confuse the sight of by means of excessive brightness.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Dazzled</b> by the headlights of the lorry, the deer stopped in the middle of the street.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1667</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton">John Milton</a>,  “Book 9”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Paradise Lost">Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a>. A Poem Written in Ten Books</a></cite>, London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title=" | Printed by | ">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>  | <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Simmons" class="extiw" title="w:Samuel Simmons">Samuel Simmons</a> | ,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and are to be sold by Peter Parker under Creed Church neer Aldgate; And by Robert Boulter at the Turks Head in Bishopsgate-street; And Matthias Walker, under St. Dunstons Church in Fleet-street">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/228722708">228722708</a></small> |  republished as  <cite>Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a> in Ten Books:<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="The Text Exactly Reproduced from the First Edition of 1667: With an Appendix Containing the Additions Made in Later Issues and a Monograph on the Original Publication of the Poem">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, London |  <a href = vnd.unilang:basil.html>Basil</a> Montagu Pickering<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="196 Piccadilly">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, 1873, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/230729554">230729554</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Those heavenly shapes / Will <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></b> now the earthly, with their blaze / Insufferably bright.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1834</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Taylor_(dramatist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Taylor (dramatist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a></a>,  <cite>Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Artevelde</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=ugUJAAAAQAAJamp;dq=dazzleamp;pg=PA45v=onepage">[1]</a></sup>, volume 1, page 45:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">An unreflected light <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> never yet / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>Dazzle</a></b> the vision feminine.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To render incapable of thinking clearly; to overwhelm with showiness or brilliance.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">impress</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">overpower</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The delegates <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b>dazzled</b> by the originality of his arguments.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be overpowered by light; to be confused by excess of brightness.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1626</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Bacon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Francis Bacon">Francis Bacon</a>,  <cite>Sylva Sylvarum: or, A Natural History in Ten Centuries</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/sylvasylvarumorn00baco/page/188">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">For <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> see, that an over-light maketh the <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>Eyes</a> <b>dazel</b>, insomuch as perpetual <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> against the Sun, would cause blindness.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1675</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aureng-zebe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Aureng-zebe">Aureng-zebe: A Tragedy</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=BudiAAAAcAAJamp;dq=dazleamp;pg=PA61v=onepage">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[…] I dare not trust these <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>Eyes</a>; / They Dance in Mists, and <b>dazle</b> with surprize.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dazzler</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dazzlement</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">endazzle</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">endazzlement</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dazzles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A light of dazzling brilliancy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Showy brilliance that may <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> a person from thinking clearly.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A herd of <a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a>.
<ul><li><b>1958</b>, Laurens <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Post, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> world of the Kalahari: with the great and the little memory</i> (<b>1998</b> David Coulson edition):
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> trying to stalk a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a> which flashed in and out of a long strip of green and yellow fever trees, with an ostrich, its <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> flared like a <a href = vnd.unilang:ballet.html>ballet</a> skirt around its dancing <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>, on their flank, when suddenly <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:darren.html>Darren</a> Paul Shearer,  <cite>In You <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> Trusts</cite>, page 176:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Zebras move in herds which are known as "dazzles." When a lion approaches a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></b> of zebras during its hunt, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Douglas Rogers,  <cite>The Last Resort: A Memoir of Mischief and Mayhem on a Family Farm in Africa</cite>, page 22:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I reached the lodge as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></b> of zebras trotted across the dirt road into thorny scrub by the game fence, and a lone kudu gazed up at <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> from the short grass near the swimming pool.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>Dazzle</a> camouflage.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">group of zebras</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">herd</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">zeal</span>.</li></ul>

***dean.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a> (2964)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deen.html>deen</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">deien</i> (which became doyen in modern French), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">decānus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deans.html>deans</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A senior official in a college or university, who may be in charge of a division or faculty (for example, the <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a> of science</i>) or have some other advisory or disciplinary function (for example, the <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a> of students</i>).</li>
<li>A dignitary or presiding officer in certain church <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a>, especially an ecclesiastical dignitary, subordinate to a bishop, in charge of a chapter of canons.</li>
<li>The senior member of some group of people.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a></b> of the diplomatic corps</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> a country's most senior ambassador</dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a></b> of the House</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> the longest-serving member of a legislature</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1955</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rex_Stout" class="extiw" title="w:Rex Stout"><a href = vnd.unilang:rex.html>Rex</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>Stout</a></a>, "The Next Witness", in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Three_Witnesses_(book)" class="extiw" title="w:Three Witnesses (book)"><i>Three Witnesses</i></a>, October 1994 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bantam_Books" class="extiw" title="w:Bantam Books">Bantam</a> edition, →ISBN, page 67:
<dl><dd>All of the switchboard operators <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> parties to it, including <a href = vnd.unilang:marie.html>Marie</a> Willis. Their <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alice.html>Alice</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>Hart</a>, collected<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
</ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Head of cathedral chapter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">provost</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a> and chapter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">deanery</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">deaness</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">decanal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">doyen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deans.html>deans</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">deaning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">deaned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To serve as a <a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To send (a student) to see the <a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>dean</a> of a university.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sussex_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Sussex dialect">Sussex</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly in place names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hill.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:debat.html>debat</a> (7197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:debiel.html>debiel</a> (7752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">débile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dēbilis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:debiel.html>debiel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:debiel.html>debieler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">debielst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mildly mentally disabled <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formally, with an IQ ranging from 50 to 80</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">stupid</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiotic</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">weak</span>, lacking strength or capacity</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:debiel.html>debiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:debielen.html>debielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:debiel.html>debieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person with a mild mental disability <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formally, with an IQ ranging from 50 to 80</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">imbecile</span></li></ol>

***deceptie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deceptie.html>deceptie</a> (107775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:deceptie.html>deceptie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deceit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deceptie.html>deceptie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deceptie.html>decepties</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">disappointment</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">disillusion</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">quality of being disappointed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teleurstelling.html>teleurstelling</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>something that causes disappointment

***decimeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:decimeren.html>decimeren</a> (76499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">décimer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:decimeren.html>decimeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decimate, to weaken</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:decoderen.html>decoderen</a> (23875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">decode</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:decoderen.html>decoderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decode, transpose a coded message in (intel)legible form</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to apply technological reversal of encryption, e.g. convert a compressed signal into the final (and original) form</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:decoratie.html>decoratie</a> (22587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">deerlike</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deerne.html>deerne</a> (65479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dierne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thiorna</i> (attested in the genitive case as <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thierno</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þewernǭ</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deerne.html>deerne</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deernen.html>deernen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deernes.html>deernes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deerne.html>deerntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">endearing  in some areas<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory  in others</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">girl</span></li>

<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> current in the eastern Netherlands. <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>Speakers</a> from other areas, especially the Randstad, may consider the term old-fashioned or literary.</li></ul>

***dees.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dees.html>dees</a> (32716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">deist</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">daz</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">ist</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">es sei denn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it be then</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the use of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></i> to introduce a specification or additional requirement.
</p><p>Alternatives include some formation with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">ees</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">once, sometime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:eins.html>eins</a></i>, or possibly a contraction similar to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tenzij.html>tenzij</a></i>, based on Middle High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">et</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">sī</i> (“it be not”), where the loss of the stressed final syllable would be unexpected, however.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:dees.html>dees</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>unless</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to do, to make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
